# LoCoBench-Agent Task

## Overview

**Task ID**: csharp_blockchain_defi_expert_070_architectural_understanding_expert_01
**Category**: architectural_understanding
**Difficulty**: expert
**Language**: csharp
**Context Length**: 916981 tokens
**Files**: 77

## Task Title

Propose Architectural Refactoring to Decouple Services with an External Message Broker

## Description

The UtilityChain Core Suite is a modular monolith designed for a new blockchain network. Its internal components (Staking, Governance, Transaction Processing, etc.) communicate via an event-driven mechanism, as documented in ADR-003. The current implementation uses a synchronous, in-memory event bus (`InMemoryEventBus`). As the platform prepares for a mainnet launch with anticipated high transaction volume and the addition of complex DeFi protocols, the core architects have identified this in-memory bus as a critical future bottleneck. It creates tight temporal coupling, is a single point of failure within each node, and prevents individual services from being scaled or updated independently. The goal is to evaluate and propose a migration to a more robust, scalable, and resilient communication architecture using an external message broker.

## Your Task

You are a senior solutions architect tasked with de-risking the UtilityChain's inter-service communication model. Your analysis should result in a technical design proposal in Markdown format.

1.  **Analyze the Current Architecture:** Examine the existing codebase and documentation (`adr/003-event-driven-module-communication.md`, `IEventBus.cs`, `InMemoryEventBus.cs`, etc.) to fully understand the current event-driven communication pattern.
2.  **Identify Key Stakeholders:** Identify all the major services/modules within the `UtilityChainCoreSuite` that currently publish or subscribe to events using the `IEventBus`.
3.  **Create a Technical Design Proposal:** Write a detailed Markdown report (`PROPOSAL.md`) that outlines a migration plan from the `InMemoryEventBus` to a persistent, external message broker (e.g., RabbitMQ, Kafka, or Azure Service Bus).

Your proposal must specifically address the following critical points:

*   **Affected Components:** List the specific services that will require modification and briefly describe the nature of the changes.
*   **Asynchronicity and Data Consistency:** The current bus is synchronous. A truly asynchronous, external broker introduces challenges with transactional guarantees. How do you ensure that a state-modifying operation (e.g., processing a transaction) and the publication of its corresponding event are atomic? Propose a specific design pattern (e.g., Transactional Outbox Pattern) to maintain data consistency across service boundaries.
*   **Configuration and Dependency Management:** Detail the necessary changes to configuration files (`appsettings.json`) and the application's startup and dependency injection logic (`Startup.cs`, `Program.cs`) to integrate the new message broker client.
*   **Resilience and Error Handling:** What new failure modes does an external broker introduce (e.g., network partitions, broker downtime, poison messages)? Propose a robust error-handling strategy, including mechanisms like dead-letter queues (DLQs) and retry policies.
*   **Architectural Trade-offs:** Conclude with a summary of the pros (e.g., scalability, resilience, decoupling) and cons (e.g., increased operational complexity, latency, new infrastructure dependency) of your proposed solution.

## Expected Approach

An expert developer would approach this task systematically:
1.  **Documentation Review:** Start by reading `docs/architecture.md` to get a high-level overview, followed by a deep dive into `docs/adr/003-event-driven-module-communication.md` to understand the intent and design of the eventing system.
2.  **Interface and Implementation Analysis:** Locate and study `src/UtilityChain.Core/Abstractions/IEventBus.cs` to understand the contract for eventing. Then, analyze `src/UtilityChain.Core/Services/InMemoryEventBus.cs` to see how its synchronous, in-memory nature is implemented (likely a simple loop through registered handlers).
3.  **Impact Analysis (Code Search):** Perform a repository-wide search for usages of `IEventBus`. This will reveal all publishers (those injecting and calling `PublishAsync`) and subscribers (those injecting and calling `Subscribe`). Key files to inspect would include `StakingService.cs`, `GovernanceService.cs`, `TransactionProcessor.cs`, and `P2PService.cs`.
4.  **Problem Formulation:** Synthesize the findings to articulate why the synchronous `InMemoryEventBus` is problematic. The key issue is that a state change and its event publication happen atomically in the same process, which is simple but not scalable or resilient. An external broker breaks this atomicity.
5.  **Solution Design (The Hard Part):** The core of the task is solving the consistency problem. The expert would identify the need for the **Transactional Outbox Pattern**. This involves:
    a.  Modifying services like `TransactionProcessor` to save the business entity (e.g., update `WorldState`) AND an `OutgoingEvent` record to the same database/state store within the *same transaction*.
    b.  Proposing a new background service/worker that polls the 'outbox' table for unpublished events and reliably sends them to the external message broker. This ensures an event is published *if and only if* the original transaction was successful.
6.  **Fleshing out the Proposal:** Based on the design, the developer would draft the Markdown report, addressing each point from the prompt with specific examples from the codebase.
    *   For configuration, they'd add a `MessageBroker` section to `appsettings.json`.
    *   For startup, they'd show how `services.AddSingleton<IEventBus, InMemoryEventBus>()` in `Startup.cs` would be replaced by a new `RabbitMQEventBus` implementation and the necessary client registration.
    *   For error handling, they would explicitly mention configuring dead-letter queues on the broker and implementing retry logic (e.g., using a library like Polly) in the event publishing and consumption code.

## Evaluation Criteria

- correctly_identifies_event_bus_usage: Accurately lists the key services that publish and subscribe to the IEventBus.
- understands_current_architecture_limitations: Clearly articulates why the synchronous, in-memory event bus is a scalability and resilience risk.
- addresses_asynchronous_consistency_challenge: Identifies the atomicity problem and proposes a robust pattern like the Transactional Outbox to solve it. This is a critical criterion.
- proposes_concrete_config_and_startup_changes: Provides specific, correct examples of changes required in `appsettings.json` and `Startup.cs`.
- analyzes_new_failure_modes_and_resilience: Demonstrates foresight by identifying new risks (broker failure, poison messages) and proposing standard solutions (DLQs, retries).
- evaluates_architectural_tradeoffs: Presents a balanced view of the pros and cons of the proposed architectural change.
- report_clarity_and_structure: The final Markdown proposal is well-organized, clearly written, and follows the requested structure.

     1→```markdown
     2→# ADR-003: Event-Driven Module Communication
     3→UtilityChain Core Suite  
     4→Created: 2024-05-26  
     5→Status: **Accepted**
     6→
     7→---
     8→
     9→## 1. Context
    10→UtilityChain is delivered as a single, self-contained .NET 8 executable.  
    11→Although a monolith, it is _modular_: **Staking**, **Consensus**, **Governance**, **Token/NFT Tooling**, and the **Smart-Contract Engine** are developed as pluggable components that must interoperate without compile-time coupling.
    12→
    13→Key forces:
    14→
    15→| Force | Explanation |
    16→|-------|-------------|
    17→| Runtime Efficiency | Blockchain nodes must achieve deterministic, micro-second latency. |
    18→| Hot-swappability  | New consensus engines, staking algorithms, or NFT standards may be introduced without shutting down a node. |
    19→| Isolation         | A failure in one module (e.g., a buggy smart-contract) must not crash the entire node. |
    20→| Observability     | Administrators need fine-grained telemetry (audit, tracing, metrics) for each module. |
    21→
    22→Traditional approaches (direct method calls, REST gRPC, message brokers) either introduce undesirable coupling or unacceptable latency.  
    23→Therefore, an **in-process event bus** (mediator) will be the spine of module communication.
    24→
    25→---
    26→
    27→## 2. Decision
    28→1. Adopt a lightweight, in-memory **Domain Event Bus** that follows the _Mediator_ and _Observer_ patterns.  
    29→2. Events are C# records implementing the `IApplicationEvent` marker interface to ensure immutability and serialization safety.  
    30→3. Modules interact exclusively through events and **Application Commands**; no module holds a hard reference to another.  
    31→4. Subs
... (truncated)

     2→# UtilityChain Core Suite – Architecture Guide
     3→_Blockchain & DeFi Utility Framework_  
     4→Version: **1.0**  
     5→Target Framework: **.NET 8**  
     6→Author: Core Engineering Team
     7→
     8→---
     9→
    10→## 1. Design Philosophy
    11→UtilityChain is a **monolithic executable** that embraces modular design through
    12→well-defined internal contracts (interfaces) and **in-process** event dispatching.
    13→This hybrid approach provides:
    14→- **Single-binary deployment** – zero external dependencies beyond .NET 8.
    15→- **Zero-copy data-flow** – shared memory models outperform gRPC/HTTP hops.
    16→- **Deterministic upgrades** – state migrations occur within the same address
    17→  space, eliminating cross-service version skews.
    18→- **Pluggable subsystems** – `IConsensusEngine`, `IGovernancePolicy`,
    19→  `ITokenStandard`, etc., are hot-swappable via the Factory/Strategy pattern.
    20→
    21→> **NOTE:** The project intentionally **does not** target public-chain
    22→> interoperability. Its primary audience is private or consortium deployments
    23→> that value operational ownership over maximal decentralization.
    24→
    25→---

I have completed the technical design proposal. Let me provide a summary of the key findings and the solution.

## Summary

I have analyzed the UtilityChain Core Suite codebase and produced a comprehensive technical design proposal for migrating from the `InMemoryEventBus` to an external message broker. The proposal has been written to `/logs/agent/solution.md`.

### Key Findings from the Analysis:

1. **Current Architecture (ADR-003)**: The system uses a lightweight, in-memory Domain Event Bus following Mediator/Observer patterns, designed for zero-copy in-process communication with sub-millisecond latency.

2. **IEventBus Implementations**: Found multiple interface definitions across the codebase reflecting the modular monolith architecture:
   - `src/UtilityChain.Core/Abstractions/IEventBus.cs`
   - `src/UtilityChain.Core/Services/InMemoryEventBus.cs` - uses `System.Threading.Channels` with multi-dispatcher model

3. **Affected Services** (Publishers):
   - **StakingService** (`StakingService.cs:31,50,93,136,208`) - publishes stake events
   - **GovernanceService** (`GovernanceService.cs:36,44,80,130,199`) - publishes proposal/vote events
   - **TransactionProcessor** (`TransactionProcessor.cs:29,43,125,134,163`) - critical path for transaction events
   - **P2PService** (`P2PService.cs:34,44,240,268,348`) - network events
   - **TokenService** (`TokenService.cs:27,39,63,98`) - token operation events
   - **ConsensusContext** (`ConsensusContext.cs:41,58,235`) - block/consensus events
   - **WorldState** (`WorldState.cs:140,152,284`) - state commit events
   - **GatewayController** (`GatewayController.cs:21,28,91,161,196`) - API gateway events

4. **Configuration**: Current `appsettings.json` at `src/UtilityChain.Node/appsettings.json:97-103` already has an `EventBus`
... (truncated)

Input
{

Output
{
  "file": {
    "content": "```markdown\n# ADR-003: Event-Driven Module Communication\nUtilityChain Core Suite  \nCreated: 2024-05-26  \nStatus: **Accepted**\n\n---\n\n## 1. Context\nUtilityChain is delivered as a single, self-contained .NET 8 executable.  \nAlthough a monolith, it is _modular_: **Staking**, **Consensus**, **Governance**, **Token/NFT Tooling**, and the **Smart-Contract Engine** are developed as pluggable components that must interoperate without compile-time coupling.\n\nKey forces:\n\n| Force | Explanation |\n|-------|-------------|\n| Runtime Efficiency | Blockchain nodes must achieve deterministic, micro-second latency. |\n| Hot-swappability  | New consensus engines, staking algorithms, or NFT standards may be introduced without shutting down a node. |\n| Isolation         | A failure in one module (e.g., a buggy smart-contract) must not crash the entire node. |\n| Observability     | Administrators need fine-grained telemetry (audit, tracing, metrics) for each module. |\n\nTraditional approaches (direct method calls, REST gRPC, message brokers) either introduce undesirable coupling or unacceptable latency.  \nTherefore, an **in-process event bus** (mediator) will be the spine of module communication.\n\n---\n\n## 2. Decision\n1. Adopt a lightweight, in-memory **Domain Event Bus** that follows the _Mediator_ and _Observer_ patterns.  \n2. Events are C# records implementing the `IApplicationEvent` marker interface to ensure immutability and serialization safety.  \n3. Modules interact exclusively through events and **Application Commands**; no module holds a hard reference to another.  \n4. Subscriptions are registered at runtime through a **Fluent Subscription API** allowing hot-plug and graceful unloading.  \n5. The bus supports:\n   \u2022 Synchronous \u201cfire-and-forget\u201d events  \n   \u2022 Asynchronous events with `Task` pipelines  \n   \u2022 Cancellation tokens for long-running work  \n   \u2022 Weak references to prevent memory leaks  \n6. Observability is baked in via the `IEventTracer` abstraction; a default OpenTelemetry implementation ships with the core suite.  \n\n---\n\n## 3. Consequences\n\u2714  Runtime coupling is reduced to the event contract; modules evolve independently.  \n\u2714  Zero-copy, in-process dispatch keeps latency in the sub-millisecond range.  \n\u2714  New modules may be loaded via reflection or MEF without recompilation.  \n\u2716  Debugging becomes harder because control-flow is no longer explicit in the call-stack.  \n\u2716  Misuse of long-running handlers can still block the thread if not awaited or scheduled correctly.  \n\n---\n\n## 4. Implementation Sketch (Production-Quality C#)\n\n```csharp\nusing System.Collections.Concurrent;\nusing System.Diagnostics;\nusing System.Diagnostics.CodeAnalysis;\nusing System.Runtime.CompilerServices;\n\nnamespace UtilityChain.Core.Eventing;\n\n/// <summary>\n/// Marker interface for immutable domain events that flow through the in-process event bus.\n/// </summary>\npublic interface IApplicationEvent { }\n\n/// <summary>\n/// A canonical contract for consuming <typeparamref name=\"TEvent\" /> messages.\n/// Handlers should be stateless and idempotent.  \n/// </summary>\npublic interface IEventHandler<in TEvent> where TEvent : IApplicationEvent\n{\n    /// <summary>Handle an application event.</summary>\n    ValueTask HandleAsync(TEvent @event, CancellationToken ct);\n}\n\n/// <summary>\n/// A handle that allows the subscriber to dispose/unsubscribe at runtime.\n/// </summary>\npublic sealed class Subscription : IDisposable\n{\n    private readonly Action _dispose;\n    private int _disposed;\n\n    internal Subscription(Action dispose) => _dispose = dispose;\n\n    public void Dispose()\n    {\n        if (Interlocked.Exchange(ref _disposed, 1) == 0)\n            _dispose();\n    }\n}\n\n/// <summary>\n/// Core implementation of the event bus.  It is intentionally lightweight, allocation-free for the hot-path,\n/// and free of third-party dependencies so that it can operate in AOT contexts.\n/// </summary>\npublic sealed class EventBus : IEventTracer\n{\n    // Handlers are stored in a thread-safe dictionary keyed by event type.\n    private readonly ConcurrentDictionary<Type, ConcurrentBag<WeakReference<object>>> _handlers = new();\n\n    // External tracer for observability; can be swapped for OpenTelemetry/Jaeger/etc.\n    private readonly IEventTracer _tracer;\n\n    public EventBus(IEventTracer? tracer = null)\n    {\n        _tracer = tracer ?? this; // Fallback to self-logging.\n    }\n\n    #region Publish\n\n    /// <summary>\n    /// Publish an event in a fire-and-forget manner.\n    /// </summary>\n    public void Publish<TEvent>(TEvent @event) where TEvent : IApplicationEvent\n        => PublishAsync(@event, CancellationToken.None).GetAwaiter().GetResult();\n\n    /// <summary>\n    /// Publish an event asynchronously.  Handlers are awaited _concurrently_.\n    /// </summary>\n    public async ValueTask PublishAsync<TEvent>(\n        TEvent @event,\n        CancellationToken ct = default) where TEvent : IApplicationEvent\n    {\n        if (_handlers.TryGetValue(typeof(TEvent), out var list))\n        {\n            var tasks = new List<ValueTask>(list.Count);\n            foreach (var weak in list)\n            {\n                if (weak.TryGetTarget(out var target) &&\n                    target is IEventHandler<TEvent> handler)\n                {\n                    tasks.Add(InvokeHandler(handler, @event, ct));\n                }\n            }\n            await ValueTask.WhenAll(tasks);\n        }\n        else\n        {\n            _tracer.TraceNoHandler(@event);\n        }\n    }\n\n    [MethodImpl(MethodImplOptions.AggressiveInlining)]\n    private async ValueTask InvokeHandler<TEvent>(\n        IEventHandler<TEvent> handler,\n        TEvent @event,\n        CancellationToken ct) where TEvent : IApplicationEvent\n    {\n        var sw = Stopwatch.StartNew();\n        try\n        {\n            await handler.HandleAsync(@event, ct).ConfigureAwait(false);\n            _tracer.TraceSuccess(@event, handler, sw.Elapsed);\n        }\n        catch (OperationCanceledException) when (ct.IsCancellationRequested)\n        {\n            _tracer.TraceCancelled(@event, handler, sw.Elapsed);\n            throw;\n        }\n        catch (Exception ex)\n        {\n            _tracer.TraceFailure(@event, handler, sw.Elapsed, ex);\n            throw;\n        }\n    }\n\n    #endregion\n\n    #region Subscribe\n\n    /// <summary>\n    /// Subscribe an <see cref=\"IEventHandler{TEvent}\" /> instance to the bus.\n    /// Returns a <see cref=\"Subscription\" /> that can be disposed to unsubscribe.\n    /// </summary>\n    public Subscription Subscribe<TEvent>(IEventHandler<TEvent> handler)\n        where TEvent : IApplicationEvent\n    {\n        var bag = _handlers.GetOrAdd(typeof(TEvent), _ => new ConcurrentBag<WeakReference<object>>());\n        var weak = new WeakReference<object>(handler);\n        bag.Add(weak);\n\n        return new Subscription(() => RemoveHandler(typeof(TEvent), weak));\n    }\n\n    private void RemoveHandler(Type type, WeakReference<object> weak)\n    {\n        if (_handlers.TryGetValue(type, out var list))\n        {\n            // ConcurrentBag does not support removal; rebuild without the disposed handler.\n            var newBag = new ConcurrentBag<WeakReference<object>>(list.Where(wr => wr != weak));\n            _handlers[type] = newBag;\n        }\n    }\n\n    #endregion\n\n    #region Self-Trace (No-op)\n\n    void IEventTracer.TraceNoHandler(IApplicationEvent ev) { }\n    void IEventTracer.TraceSuccess(IApplicationEvent ev, object handler, TimeSpan dur) { }\n    void IEventTracer.TraceCancelled(IApplicationEvent ev, object handler, TimeSpan dur) { }\n    void IEventTracer.TraceFailure(IApplicationEvent ev, object handler, TimeSpan dur, Exception ex) { }\n\n    #endregion\n}\n\n/// <summary>\n/// Defines tracing callbacks for diagnostics.  Implementations should be side-effect-free.\n/// </summary>\npublic interface IEventTracer\n{\n    void TraceNoHandler(IApplicationEvent ev);\n    void TraceSuccess(IApplicationEvent ev, object handler, TimeSpan dur);\n    void TraceCancelled(IApplicationEvent ev, object handler, TimeSpan dur);\n    void TraceFailure(IApplicationEvent ev, object handler, TimeSpan dur, Exception ex);\n}\n```\n\n### Usage Example\n\n```csharp\n// 1. Create a concrete event\npublic sealed record TokensMinted(Guid TokenId, decimal Amount, Address Owner) : IApplicationEvent;\n\n// 2. Implement a handler that reacts to the event\npublic sealed class LedgerProjection : IEventHandler<TokensMinted>\n{\n    private readonly ILedgerRepository _repo;\n    public LedgerProjection(ILedgerRepository repo) => _repo = repo;\n\n    public async ValueTask HandleAsync(TokensMinted e, CancellationToken ct)\n    {\n        var entry = new LedgerEntry(e.TokenId, e.Owner, e.Amount, LedgerOp.Mint);\n        await _repo.AddAsync(entry, ct);\n    }\n}\n\n// 3. Wire up in the composition root\nvar bus = new EventBus(new OpenTelemetryTracer());\nvar projection = new LedgerProjection(repo);\nusing var sub = bus.Subscribe(projection);\n\n// 4. Somewhere in the Token module\u2026\nawait bus.PublishAsync(new TokensMinted(tokenId, 250, caller.Address), ct);\n```\n\n---\n\n## 5. Future Work\n\u2022 Integrate a deterministic, priority-aware scheduler so that consensus-critical events pre-empt UI telemetry.  \n\u2022 Provide Roslyn source generators for boiler-plate handler registration.  \n\u2022 Investigate out-of-process fallbacks (e.g., NATS, Kafka) for horizontally scaled, multi-process deployments.\n\n---\n\u00a9 2024 UtilityChain Contributors \u2013 Released under the MIT License\n```",

Design Philosophy\nUtilityChain is a **monolithic executable** that embraces modular design through\nwell-defined internal contracts (interfaces) and **in-process** event dispatching.\nThis hybrid approach provides:\n- **Single-binary deployment** \u2013 zero external dependencies beyond .NET 8.\n- **Zero-copy data-flow** \u2013 shared memory models outperform gRPC/HTTP hops.\n- **Deterministic upgrades** \u2013 state migrations occur within the same address\n  space, eliminating cross-service version skews.\n- **Pluggable subsystems** \u2013 `IConsensusEngine`, `IGovernancePolicy`,\n  `ITokenStandard`, etc., are hot-swappable via the Factory/Strategy pattern.\n\n> **NOTE:** The project intentionally **does not** target public-chain\n> interoperability. Its primary audience is private or consortium deployments\n> that value operational ownership over maximal decentralization.\n\n---\n\n## 2. High-Level Component Map\n\n```mermaid\nflowchart LR\n    subgraph CLI & UI\n        CLI[Command Line Tooling]\n        WalletDesktop[Desktop Wallet]\n        IDE[Smart-Contract IDE]\n    end\n    subgraph API Gateway\n        REST[REST Controller]\n        GraphQL[GraphQL Controller]\n    end\n    subgraph Core Engine\n        EventBus\n        StateMgr[State Machine Coordinator]\n        Ledger[UTXO / Account Ledger]\n        SmartVM[Smart-Contract VM]\n        NFT[NFT Toolkit]\n        Token[Token Toolkit]\n        Consensus[Consensus Engines]\n        Staking[Staking Module]\n        Governance[Governance Module]\n    end\n    subgraph Persist\n        RocksDb[(RocksDB)]\n        Snapshot[(Snapshot & Backup)]\n    end\n    CLI & UI -->|IPC / Localhost| API Gateway\n    API Gateway --> EventBus\n    EventBus --> StateMgr\n    StateMgr --> Ledger\n    StateMgr --> SmartVM\n    SmartVM --> Ledger\n    Staking --> Ledger\n    Consensus --> Ledger\n    Consensus --> EventBus\n    NFT --> SmartVM\n    Token --> SmartVM\n    Governance --> EventBus\n    Ledger --> RocksDb\n    Snapshot --> RocksDb\n```\n\n---\n\n## 3. Core Architectural Patterns\n\n| Pattern             | Purpose                                                           |\n|---------------------|-------------------------------------------------------------------|\n| **Event Driven**    | Decouples producers/consumers (`EventBus`)                        |\n| **State Machine**   | Linearizes multi-module state mutations (`StateCoordinator`)      |\n| **Proxy**           | Lazy-loads external cryptography providers                        |\n| **Strategy**        | Hot-swappable consensus & staking algorithms                      |\n| **Factory**         | Creates domain objects (`Block`, `Transaction`, `Token`)          |\n| **Observer**        | Real-time UI updates & monitoring                                 |\n\n---\n\n## 4. Module Specifications\n\n### 4.1 EventBus\n\n```csharp\npublic interface IEventBus\n{\n    void Publish<TEvent>(TEvent @event) where TEvent : DomainEvent;\n    IDisposable Subscribe<TEvent>(Action<TEvent> handler) where TEvent : DomainEvent;\n}\n```\n\nImplementation wraps a lock-free,\nmulti-producer \u2192 multi-consumer ring buffer (powered by\n`System.Threading.Channels`) facilitating up to **8 M msgs/sec** on commodity\nhardware.\n\n### 4.2 State Machine Coordinator\n\nResponsible for **serializing side-effect-ful transitions** (block addition,\ngovernance rule updates, staking rewards). Incoming transactions are first\nvalidated in parallel; committing them is single-threaded to guarantee a total\norder.\n\n```csharp\ninternal sealed class StateCoordinator : IAsyncDisposable\n{\n    private readonly Channel<IStateCommand> _channel =\n        Channel.CreateUnbounded<IStateCommand>(new UnboundedChannelOptions {\n            SingleReader = true,\n            SingleWriter = false\n        });\n\n    public async ValueTask<IStateResult> EnqueueAsync(IStateCommand cmd,\n                                                      CancellationToken ct = default)\n    {\n        await _channel.Writer.WriteAsync(cmd, ct);\n        return await cmd.Completion.Task.ConfigureAwait(false);\n    }\n\n    // Single reader task\n    private async Task RunAsync()\n    {\n        await foreach (var cmd in _channel.Reader.ReadAllAsync())\n        {\n            IStateResult result = await cmd.ExecuteAsync();\n            cmd.Completion.TrySetResult(result);\n        }\n    }\n}\n```\n\n### 4.3 Consensus Engine Strategy\n\n`ConsensusEngineFactory` selects a concrete engine at startup\n(`ProofOfAuthority`, `DPoS`, or `RaftBFT`) based on `appsettings.json` or CLI\nflag.\n\n```csharp\npublic interface IConsensusEngine\n{\n    string Name { get; }\n    ValueTask<ConsensusResult> ValidateBlockAsync(Block block, CancellationToken ct);\n    ValueTask<ConsensusResult> FinalizeBlockAsync(Block block, CancellationToken ct);\n}\n```\n\n---\n\n## 5. Data Persistence\n\n1. **RocksDB** key-value store  \n   - Column Families: `blocks`, `tx_index`, `state`, `snapshots`\n2. **Snapshot Service**  \n   - Creates LZ4-compressed snapshots every _N_ blocks.\n   - Uses Copy-on-Write to avoid write stalls.\n\n---\n\n## 6. Security Model\n\n- **Memory-hard KDF** (`Argon2id`) for wallet key encryption.\n- **Constant-time cryptographic operations** to prevent side-channel attacks.\n- **Capability-based sandbox** for Smart-Contract VM; contracts must declare\n  required capabilities (`storage.read`, `storage.write`, `token.mint`).\n\n---\n\n## 7. Extensibility Guidelines\n\n1. Implement the respective interface (`IConsensusEngine`, `IStakingCalculator`,\n   etc.).\n2. Register your type in `module.json`:\n\n```json\n{\n  \"consensus\": \"MyCompany.UtilityChain.PowEngine, MyCompany.UtilityChain\"\n}\n```\n\n3. Rebuild the monolith:  \n   `dotnet publish -c Release -r linux-x64 --single-file`\n\n---\n\n## 8. Build & Deployment\n\n```bash\n# Build\ndotnet restore\ndotnet build -c Release\n\n# Publish self-contained executable\ndotnet publish -c Release -r win-x64 --self-contained true /p:PublishSingleFile=true\n```\n\nThe resulting binary (`utilitychain.exe` or `utilitychain`) is the only file\nrequired on the target host.\n\n---\n\n## 9. Observability\n\n- **Structured logging** via `Serilog` to Console, File, Seq.\n- **Metrics** exposed on `/metrics` (Prometheus).\n- **Health Checks** (`/health/live`, `/health/ready`).\n\n---\n\n## 10. Appendix\n\n### 10.1 Transaction Commit Sequence\n\n```mermaid\nsequenceDiagram\n    participant UI\n    participant API\n    participant EventBus\n    participant StateCoord\n    participant Ledger\n    participant Rocks\n\n    UI->>API: POST /tx\n    API->>EventBus: Publish(TxSubmitted)\n    EventBus->>StateCoord: Dispatch(AddTxCommand)\n    StateCoord->>Ledger: Validate() / Apply()\n    Ledger->>Rocks: Persist()\n    StateCoord-->>EventBus: Publish(TxCommitted)\n    EventBus-->>API: Push(TxCommitted)\n    API-->>UI: HTTP 202 + WebSocket stream\n```\n\n---\n\n\u00a9 2024 UtilityChain Core Suite  \nThis document is licensed under the MIT License.\n```",

See LICENSE file in the root directory for more\n//  information.\n// -----------------------------------------------------------------------------\n//  File:        InMemoryEventBus.cs\n//  Description: High-performance in-process event bus for decoupled module\n//               communication inside the monolithic UtilityChain executable.\n//  ---------------------------------------------------------------------------\n\n#nullable enable\nusing System.Collections.Concurrent;\nusing System.Diagnostics;\nusing System.Diagnostics.CodeAnalysis;\nusing System.Runtime.CompilerServices;\nusing System.Threading.Channels;\nusing Microsoft.Extensions.Logging;\n\nnamespace UtilityChain.Core.Services;\n\n/// <summary>\n/// Marker interface for events flowing through <see cref=\"InMemoryEventBus\" />.\n/// </summary>\npublic interface IEvent { }\n\n/// <summary>\n/// Event bus contract used throughout the UtilityChain codebase. Only in-process\n/// communication is required; therefore implementations may rely on shared\n/// memory and do not need to provide distributed guarantees.\n/// </summary>\npublic interface IEventBus : IAsyncDisposable, IDisposable\n{\n    /// <summary>\n    /// Subscribes to events of type <typeparamref name=\"TEvent\" />.\n    /// </summary>\n    /// <param name=\"handler\">\n    /// Asynchronous delegate invoked when an event is published.\n    /// </param>\n    /// <param name=\"subscriberId\">\n    /// Optional friendly identifier used for logging and unsubscription.\n    /// </param>\n    /// <typeparam name=\"TEvent\">Concrete event type.</typeparam>\n    /// <returns>\n    /// An <see cref=\"IDisposable\" /> that should be disposed to remove the\n    /// subscription.\n    /// </returns>\n    IDisposable Subscribe<TEvent>(\n        Func<TEvent, CancellationToken, ValueTask> handler,\n        string? subscriberId = null)\n        where TEvent : IEvent;\n\n    /// <summary>\n    /// Publishes an event to the bus. The call is non-blocking; the event is\n    /// enqueued and processed on background dispatchers respecting ordering.\n    /// </summary>\n    /// <typeparam name=\"TEvent\">Concrete event type.</typeparam>\n    /// <param name=\"event\">The event instance.</param>\n    /// <param name=\"cancellationToken\">\n    /// Token that propagates cancellation to observers.\n    /// </param>\n    ValueTask PublishAsync<TEvent>(\n        TEvent @event,\n        CancellationToken cancellationToken = default)\n        where TEvent : IEvent;\n\n    /// <summary>\n    /// Checks if the bus currently has any subscribers for <paramref name=\"eventType\"/>.\n    /// </summary>\n    bool HasSubscribers(Type eventType);\n}\n\n/// <summary>\n/// High-performance, lock-free in-memory event bus optimized for a modular\n/// monolith. The implementation uses <see cref=\"System.Threading.Channels\"/>\n/// to guarantee FIFO ordering, back-pressure and bounded concurrency.\n/// </summary>\npublic sealed class InMemoryEventBus : IEventBus\n{\n    private readonly ILogger<InMemoryEventBus> _logger;\n    private readonly int _dispatcherCount;\n    private readonly Channel<EventEnvelope> _channel;\n    private readonly CancellationTokenSource _cts = new();\n    private readonly Task[] _dispatchers;\n\n    // Map: EventType -> (SubscriberId -> Subscription)\n    private readonly ConcurrentDictionary<Type,\n        ConcurrentDictionary<string, Subscription>> _subscriptions = new();\n\n    // Used when the caller does not specify a subscriberId.\n    private static long _autoIncrementSubscriberId;\n\n    private bool _disposed;\n\n    /// <summary>\n    /// Creates a new instance with the provided logger. Dispatcher thread-count\n    /// defaults to <c>Environment.ProcessorCount</c>.\n    /// </summary>\n    public InMemoryEventBus(\n        ILogger<InMemoryEventBus> logger,\n        int? dispatcherCount = null,\n        int channelCapacity = 65_536)\n    {\n        _logger = logger ?? throw new ArgumentNullException(nameof(logger));\n\n        _dispatcherCount = dispatcherCount is > 0 ? dispatcherCount.Value : Environment.ProcessorCount;\n        var options = new BoundedChannelOptions(channelCapacity)\n        {\n            SingleReader = false,\n            SingleWriter = false,\n            FullMode = BoundedChannelFullMode.Wait\n        };\n        _channel = Channel.CreateBounded<EventEnvelope>(options);\n\n        // Spin up background dispatcher tasks.\n        _dispatchers = new Task[_dispatcherCount];\n        for (var i = 0; i < _dispatcherCount; i++)\n        {\n            _dispatchers[i] = Task.Factory.StartNew(\n                () => DispatcherLoop(i, _cts.Token),\n                _cts.Token,\n                TaskCreationOptions.LongRunning,\n                TaskScheduler.Default);\n        }\n\n        _logger.LogInformation(\n            \"In-memory event bus initialised with {DispatcherCount} dispatcher(s) and capacity {Capacity}\",\n            _dispatcherCount, channelCapacity);\n    }\n\n    // ---------------------------------------------------------------------\n    // IEventBus implementation\n    // ---------------------------------------------------------------------\n\n    public IDisposable Subscribe<TEvent>(\n        Func<TEvent, CancellationToken, ValueTask> handler,\n        string? subscriberId = null)\n        where TEvent : IEvent\n    {\n        if (handler is null) throw new ArgumentNullException(nameof(handler));\n\n        var type = typeof(TEvent);\n        var id = subscriberId ?? $\"auto_{Interlocked.Increment(ref _autoIncrementSubscriberId)}\";\n\n        var subscriberMap = _subscriptions.GetOrAdd(type,\n            _ => new ConcurrentDictionary<string, Subscription>());\n\n        var subscription = new Subscription(this, type, id,\n            async (obj, token) =>\n            {\n                // Fast cast without 'as' to keep boxing minimal.\n                await handler(Unsafe.As<TEvent>(obj), token).ConfigureAwait(false);\n            });\n\n        if (!subscriberMap.TryAdd(id, subscription))\n        {\n            throw new InvalidOperationException(\n                $\"A subscriber with id '{id}' is already registered for events of type '{type.Name}'.\");\n        }\n\n        _logger.LogDebug(\n            \"Subscriber '{SubscriberId}' registered for event type '{EventType}'\",\n            id, type.Name);\n\n        return subscription;\n    }\n\n    public async ValueTask PublishAsync<TEvent>(\n        TEvent @event,\n        CancellationToken cancellationToken = default)\n        where TEvent : IEvent\n    {\n        if (_disposed) ThrowObjectDisposed();\n\n        if (@event is null) throw new ArgumentNullException(nameof(@event));\n\n        // We still enqueue even when there are no subscribers; this allows\n        // diagnostics to track publication frequency if needed.\n        var envelope = new EventEnvelope(@event, cancellationToken);\n\n        // This can block if the bounded channel is full: built-in back-pressure.\n        await _channel.Writer.WriteAsync(envelope, cancellationToken).ConfigureAwait(false);\n    }\n\n    public bool HasSubscribers(Type eventType)\n    {\n        if (eventType is null) throw new ArgumentNullException(nameof(eventType));\n        return _subscriptions.TryGetValue(eventType, out var map) && !map.IsEmpty;\n    }\n\n    // ---------------------------------------------------------------------\n    // Housekeeping\n    // ---------------------------------------------------------------------\n\n    public void Dispose() => DisposeAsync().AsTask().GetAwaiter().GetResult();\n\n    public async ValueTask DisposeAsync()\n    {\n        if (_disposed) return;\n        _disposed = true;\n\n        _logger.LogInformation(\"Disposing in-memory event bus\u2026\");\n\n        _cts.Cancel();\n        _channel.Writer.Complete();\n\n        try\n        {\n            await Task.WhenAll(_dispatchers).ConfigureAwait(false);\n        }\n        catch (Exception ex) when (ex is TaskCanceledException or OperationCanceledException)\n        {\n            // Expected during shutdown, suppress.\n        }\n\n        _cts.Dispose();\n    }\n\n    // ---------------------------------------------------------------------\n    // Internal dispatcher logic\n    // ---------------------------------------------------------------------\n\n    private async Task DispatcherLoop(int dispatcherIndex, CancellationToken token)\n    {\n        try\n        {\n            var reader = _channel.Reader;\n            while (await reader.WaitToReadAsync(token).ConfigureAwait(false))\n            {\n                while (reader.TryRead(out var envelope))\n                {\n                    Deliver(envelope);\n                }\n            }\n        }\n        catch (OperationCanceledException)\n        {\n            // Normal on shutdown.\n        }\n        catch (Exception ex)\n        {\n            _logger.LogCritical(ex, \"Dispatcher {Index} crashed unexpectedly\", dispatcherIndex);\n        }\n    }\n\n    private void Deliver(EventEnvelope envelope)\n    {\n        if (!_subscriptions.TryGetValue(envelope.Event.GetType(), out var subscribers) ||\n            subscribers.IsEmpty)\n        {\n            // No subscribers: nothing to do.\n            return;\n        }\n\n        foreach (var sub in subscribers.Values)\n        {\n            // Fire-and-forget: each handler is executed independently.\n            _ = Task.Run(async () =>\n            {\n                var sw = ValueStopwatch.StartNew();\n                try\n                {\n                    await sub.Handler(envelope.Event, envelope.PublishCancellationToken)\n                        .ConfigureAwait(false);\n\n                    _logger.LogTrace(\n                        \"Event '{EventType}' delivered to '{SubscriberId}' in {Elapsed} \u00b5s\",\n                        envelope.Event.GetType().Name, sub.Id, sw.ElapsedMicroseconds);\n                }\n                catch (Exception ex)\n                {\n                    _logger.LogError(ex,\n                        \"Error delivering event '{EventType}' to subscriber '{SubscriberId}'\",\n                        envelope.Event.GetType().Name, sub.Id);\n                }\n            });\n        }\n    }\n\n    // ---------------------------------------------------------------------\n    // Helpers\n    // ---------------------------------------------------------------------\n\n    [MethodImpl(MethodImplOptions.NoInlining)]\n    private static void ThrowObjectDisposed() =>\n        throw new ObjectDisposedException(nameof(InMemoryEventBus));\n\n    /// <summary>\n    /// Encapsulates an event and metadata used by the dispatcher.\n    /// </summary>\n    private sealed record EventEnvelope(object Event, CancellationToken PublishCancellationToken);\n\n    /// <summary>\n    /// Represents a single subscription. Disposing removes it from the bus.\n    /// </summary>\n    private sealed class Subscription : IDisposable\n    {\n        private readonly InMemoryEventBus _bus;\n        private readonly Type _eventType;\n        private bool _isDisposed;\n\n        public string Id { get; }\n        public Func<object, CancellationToken, ValueTask> Handler { get; }\n\n        public Subscription(\n            InMemoryEventBus bus,\n            Type eventType,\n            string id,\n            Func<object, CancellationToken, ValueTask> handler)\n        {\n            _bus = bus;\n            _eventType = eventType;\n            Id = id;\n            Handler = handler;\n        }\n\n        public void Dispose()\n        {\n            if (_isDisposed) return;\n            _isDisposed = true;\n\n            if (_bus._subscriptions.TryGetValue(_eventType, out var map) &&\n                map.TryRemove(Id, out _))\n            {\n                _bus._logger.LogDebug(\n                    \"Subscriber '{SubscriberId}' removed from event type '{EventType}'\",\n                    Id, _eventType.Name);\n            }\n        }\n    }\n\n    // Fast, allocation-free stopwatch helper.\n    private readonly struct ValueStopwatch\n    {\n        private static readonly double TickFrequency =\n            1_000_000.0 / Stopwatch.Frequency; // microsecond conversion\n\n        private readonly long _start;\n\n        private ValueStopwatch(long start) => _start = start;\n\n        public static ValueStopwatch StartNew() => new(Stopwatch.GetTimestamp());\n\n        public double ElapsedMicroseconds =>\n            (Stopwatch.GetTimestamp() - _start) * TickFrequency;\n    }\n}\n```\n",

New total: {Total}.\",\n                address, amount, lockPeriod, account.TotalStaked);\n\n            _eventBus.Publish(new StakeCreatedEvent(stake, account.TotalStaked));\n\n            return new StakeReceipt(stake.StakeId, stake.CreatedAt);\n        }\n        finally\n        {\n            account.Semaphore.Release();\n        }\n    }\n\n    /// <inheritdoc />\n    public async Task<UnstakeReceipt> UnstakeAsync(\n        Address address, StakeId stakeId, CancellationToken ct = default)\n    {\n        ArgumentNullException.ThrowIfNull(address);\n        ArgumentNullException.ThrowIfNull(stakeId);\n\n        if (!_accounts.TryGetValue(address, out var account))\n            throw new StakeNotFoundException(stakeId);\n\n        await account.Semaphore.WaitAsync(ct).ConfigureAwait(false);\n        try\n        {\n            var stake = account.GetStake(stakeId);\n\n            if (stake == null)\n                throw new StakeNotFoundException(stakeId);\n\n            if (stake.State != StakeState.Locked &&\n                stake.State != StakeState.Released)\n                throw new InvalidStakeTransitionException(stake.State, StakeState.Withdrawn);\n\n            if (stake.State == StakeState.Locked &&\n                _clock.Now < stake.UnlocksAt)\n                throw new StakeLockedException(stake.UnlocksAt);\n\n            stake.State = StakeState.Withdrawn;\n            account.TotalStaked -= stake.Amount;\n\n            _logger.LogInformation(\n                \"Stake {StakeId} withdrawn. Address {Address} remaining total: {Total}.\",\n                stakeId, address, account.TotalStaked);\n\n            _eventBus.Publish(new StakeWithdrawnEvent(stake));\n\n            return new UnstakeReceipt(stake.StakeId, _clock.Now, stake.Amount);\n        }\n        finally\n        {\n            account.Semaphore.Release();\n        }\n    }\n\n    /// <inheritdoc />\n    public async Task<IReadOnlyCollection<StakeInfo>> GetStakesAsync(Address address,\n        CancellationToken ct = default)\n    {\n        ArgumentNullException.ThrowIfNull(address);\n\n        if (!_accounts.TryGetValue(address, out var account))\n            return Array.Empty<StakeInfo>();\n\n        await account.Semaphore.WaitAsync(ct).ConfigureAwait(false);\n        try\n        {\n            return account.ListStakes();\n        }\n        finally\n        {\n            account.Semaphore.Release();\n        }\n    }\n\n    /// <inheritdoc />\n    public async Task<decimal> GetAccumulatedRewardsAsync(Address address,\n        CancellationToken ct = default)\n    {\n        ArgumentNullException.ThrowIfNull(address);\n\n        if (!_accounts.TryGetValue(address, out var account))\n            return 0m;\n\n        await account.Semaphore.WaitAsync(ct).ConfigureAwait(false);\n        try\n        {\n            var rewards = _rewardCalculator.Calculate(account, _clock.Now);\n\n            return rewards;\n        }\n        finally\n        {\n            account.Semaphore.Release();\n        }\n    }\n\n    /// <inheritdoc />\n    public async Task ClaimRewardsAsync(Address address, CancellationToken ct = default)\n    {\n        ArgumentNullException.ThrowIfNull(address);\n\n        if (!_accounts.TryGetValue(address, out var account))\n            throw new StakingException(\"Account not found.\");\n\n        await account.Semaphore.WaitAsync(ct).ConfigureAwait(false);\n        try\n        {\n            var rewards = _rewardCalculator.Calculate(account, _clock.Now);\n\n            if (rewards <= 0m)\n                throw new StakingException(\"No rewards available.\");\n\n            account.RewardsClaimed += rewards;\n\n            _logger.LogInformation(\"Address {Address} claimed {Rewards} rewards\", address, rewards);\n\n            _eventBus.Publish(new RewardsClaimedEvent(address, rewards));\n        }\n        finally\n        {\n            account.Semaphore.Release();\n        }\n    }\n\n    // ---------------------------------------------------------------------\n    // Event handling\n    // ---------------------------------------------------------------------\n    // Called for every new block to update lock expirations and reward indexes\n    private void OnNewBlock(NewBlockEvent e)\n    {\n        foreach (var (_, account) in _accounts)\n        {\n            // Intentionally fire-and-forget; minimal per-block CPU time\n            _ = Task.Run(() =>\n            {\n                if (!account.Semaphore.Wait(0))\n                    return; // Skip busy accounts to maintain block throughput\n\n                try\n                {\n                    account.ProcessBlock(_clock.Now);\n                }\n                catch (Exception ex)\n                {\n                    _logger.LogError(ex, \"Failed to process staking updates for address {Address}.\",\n                        account.Address);\n                }\n                finally\n                {\n                    account.Semaphore.Release();\n                }\n            }, _cts.Token);\n        }\n    }\n\n    // ---------------------------------------------------------------------\n    // Background persistence loop\n    // ---------------------------------------------------------------------\n    private async Task BackgroundSyncLoopAsync()\n    {\n        var token = _cts.Token;\n\n        try\n        {\n            while (!token.IsCancellationRequested)\n            {\n                await Task.Delay(TimeSpan.FromMinutes(1), token).ConfigureAwait(false);\n\n                foreach (var (_, account) in _accounts)\n                {\n                    if (!account.Semaphore.Wait(0))\n                        continue; // Skip active accounts\n\n                    try\n                    {\n                        var snapshot = account.CreateSnapshot();\n                        await _repository.SaveAsync(snapshot, token).ConfigureAwait(false);\n                    }\n                    catch (Exception ex)\n                    {\n                        _logger.LogWarning(ex, \"Failed to persist staking snapshot for {Address}.\",\n                            account.Address);\n                    }\n                    finally\n                    {\n                        account.Semaphore.Release();\n                    }\n                }\n            }\n        }\n        catch (OperationCanceledException)\n        {\n            // Normal shutdown\n        }\n        catch (Exception ex)\n        {\n            _logger.LogCritical(ex, \"Unexpected failure in staking background loop.\");\n        }\n    }\n\n    // ---------------------------------------------------------------------\n    // Disposable\n    // ---------------------------------------------------------------------\n    public async ValueTask DisposeAsync()\n    {\n        _cts.Cancel();\n\n        _eventBus.Unsubscribe<NewBlockEvent>(OnNewBlock);\n\n        try\n        {\n            await _syncTask.ConfigureAwait(false);\n        }\n        catch (Exception ex)\n        {\n            _logger.LogWarning(ex, \"Failure while stopping staking service sync loop.\");\n        }\n\n        _cts.Dispose();\n    }\n\n    // #region Domain\n\n    private sealed class StakeAccount\n    {\n        private readonly ConcurrentDictionary<StakeId, Stake> _stakes = new();\n        internal readonly SemaphoreSlim Semaphore             = new(1, 1);\n\n        internal StakeAccount(Address address)\n        {\n            Address = address;\n            Created = DateTimeOffset.UtcNow;\n        }\n\n        internal Address      Address         { get; }\n        internal DateTimeOffset Created       { get; }\n        internal ulong        TotalStaked     { get; set; }\n        internal decimal      RewardsClaimed  { get; set; _stakes[stake.StakeId] = stake;\n            TotalStaked += amount;\n            return stake;\n        }\n\n        internal Stake? GetStake(StakeId id) => _stakes.TryGetValue(id, out var s) ? s : null;\n\n        internal void ProcessBlock(DateTimeOffset now)\n        {\n            foreach (var stake in _stakes.Values)\n            {\n                stake.TryRelease(now);\n            }\n        }\n\n        internal IReadOnlyCollection<StakeInfo> ListStakes()\n        {\n            var list = new List<StakeInfo>(_stakes.Count);\n            foreach (var s in _stakes.Values)\n            {\n                list.Add(s.ToInfo());\n            }\n\n            return list.AsReadOnly();\n        }\n\n        internal StakeAccountSnapshot CreateSnapshot()\n        {\n            var stakeSnapshots = new List<StakeSnapshot>();\n\n            foreach (var s in _stakes.Values)\n            {\n                stakeSnapshots.Add(new StakeSnapshot(\n                    s.StakeId,\n                    s.Amount,\n                    s.CreatedAt,\n                    s.UnlocksAt,\n                    s.State));\n            }\n\n            return new StakeAccountSnapshot(\n                Address,\n                Created,\n                TotalStaked,\n                RewardsClaimed,\n                stakeSnapshots);\n        }\n    }\n\n    private sealed class Stake\n    {\n        private static readonly RNGCryptoServiceProvider Rng = new();\n\n        internal Stake(ulong amount, DateTimeOffset createdAt, TimeSpan lockPeriod)\n        {\n            Amount    = amount;\n            CreatedAt = createdAt;\n            UnlocksAt = createdAt + lockPeriod;\n            State     = StakeState.Locked;\n            StakeId   = GenerateId();\n        }\n\n        internal ulong           Amount     { get; }\n        internal DateTimeOffset  CreatedAt  { get; }\n        internal DateTimeOffset  UnlocksAt  { get; }\n        internal StakeState      State      { get; set; }\n        internal StakeId         StakeId    { get; }\n\n        internal void TryRelease(DateTimeOffset now)\n        {\n            if (State == StakeState.Locked && now >= UnlocksAt)\n            {\n                State = StakeState.Released;\n            }\n        }\n\n        internal StakeInfo ToInfo() => new(\n            StakeId,\n            Amount,\n            CreatedAt,\n            UnlocksAt,\n            State);\n\n        private static StakeId GenerateId()\n        {\n            Span<byte> bytes = stackalloc byte[16];\n            Rng.GetBytes(bytes);\n            return new StakeId(Convert.ToHexString(bytes));\n        }\n    }\n\n    #endregion\n}\n\n// private const decimal Apr = 0.08m; // 8% APR\n\n        public decimal Calculate(object accountObj, DateTimeOffset now)\n        {\n            if (accountObj is not StakingService.StakeAccount account)\n                throw new ArgumentException(nameof(accountObj));\n\n            var secondsYear = 365 * 24 * 60 * 60;\n            var accrued     = 0m;\n\n            foreach (var stakeInfo in account.ListStakes())\n            {\n                if (stakeInfo.State == StakeState.Withdrawn)\n                    continue;\n\n                var durationSeconds = (decimal)(now - stakeInfo.CreatedAt).TotalSeconds;\n                accrued += stakeInfo.Amount * (Apr * durationSeconds / secondsYear);\n            }\n\n            return Math.Round(accrued - All rights reserved.\n// </copyright>\n// --------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------\n// ReSharper disable MemberCanBePrivate.Global\n// ReSharper disable AutoPropertyCanBeMadeGetOnly.Local\n\nusing System;\nusing System.Collections.Concurrent;\nusing System.Collections.Generic;\nusing System.Diagnostics.CodeAnalysis;\nusing System.Linq;\nusing System.Threading;\nusing System.Threading.Tasks;\nusing UtilityChain.Governance.Events;\nusing UtilityChain.Governance.Models;\nusing UtilityChain.SharedKernel.Events;\nusing UtilityChain.SharedKernel.Time;\n\nnamespace UtilityChain.Governance;\n\n/// <summary>\n///     Central orchestrator for on-chain governance.\n///     Handles proposal lifecycle, voting logic, and policy enforcement.\n///     Thread-safe and event-driven.\n/// </summary>\n/// <remarks>\n///     NOTE: This implementation keeps state in-memory. In production, persist proposals and votes to durable storage.\n/// </remarks>\npublic sealed class GovernanceService : IGovernanceService, IDisposable\n{\n    private readonly ConcurrentDictionary<Guid, ProposalAggregate> _proposals = new();\n    private readonly IEnumerable<IGovernancePolicy>               _policies;\n    private readonly IEventBus                                     _eventBus;\n    private readonly ISystemClock                                  _clock;\n    private readonly ReaderWriterLockSlim                          _lifecycleLock = new();\n\n    private bool _disposed;\n\n    public GovernanceService(\n        IEnumerable<IGovernancePolicy> policies,\n        IEventBus                      eventBus,\n        ISystemClock                   clock)\n    {\n        _policies  = policies ?? throw new ArgumentNullException(nameof(policies));\n        _eventBus  = eventBus ?? throw new ArgumentNullException(nameof(eventBus));\n        _clock     = clock   ?? throw new ArgumentNullException(nameof(clock));\n\n        // Hook up reactive listeners (Observer pattern) for downstream services\n        _eventBus.Subscribe<ProposalCreatedEvent>(OnProposalCreatedAsync);\n        _eventBus.Subscribe<ProposalFinalizedEvent>(OnProposalFinalizedAsync);\n    }\n\n    #region IGovernanceService\n\n    public Proposal CreateProposal(CreateProposalRequest request, CancellationToken ct = default)\n    {\n        ThrowIfDisposed();\n\n        if (request is null) throw new ArgumentNullException(nameof(request));\n\n        var proposal = new Proposal(\n            Guid.NewGuid(),\n            request.Title.Trim(),\n            request.Description.Trim(),\n            _clock.UtcNow,\n            request.VotingDeadline,\n            ProposalStatus.Pending);\n\n        if (!_policies.All(p => p.ValidateProposal(proposal)))\n            throw new GovernanceException(\"One or more policies rejected the proposal.\");\n\n        var aggregate = new ProposalAggregate(proposal);\n\n        if (!_proposals.TryAdd(proposal.Id, aggregate))\n            throw new InvalidOperationException($\"Proposal ID collision occurred: {proposal.Id}\");\n\n        _eventBus.Publish(new ProposalCreatedEvent(proposal));\n\n        return proposal;\n    }\n\n    public VoteReceipt CastVote(Guid proposalId, VoteType voteType, string voterAddress, CancellationToken ct = default)\n    {\n        ThrowIfDisposed();\n\n        if (string.IsNullOrWhiteSpace(voterAddress))\n            throw new ArgumentException(\"Voter address must be provided.\", nameof(voterAddress));\n\n        if (!_proposals.TryGetValue(proposalId, out var aggregate))\n            throw new ProposalNotFoundException(proposalId);\n\n        _lifecycleLock.EnterUpgradeableReadLock();\n        try\n        {\n            if (aggregate.Proposal.Status is ProposalStatus.Finalized)\n                throw new GovernanceException(\"Voting period has ended for this proposal.\");\n\n            if (aggregate.Proposal.VotingDeadline <= _clock.UtcNow)\n            {\n                // Attempt to finalize asynchronously\u2014do not block caller\n                _ = Task.Run(() => FinalizeAsync(aggregate, default), ct);\n                throw new GovernanceException(\"Voting period has already elapsed.\");\n            }\n\n            var vote = new Vote(\n                aggregate.Proposal.Id,\n                voterAddress,\n                voteType,\n                _clock.UtcNow);\n\n            if (aggregate.HasVoted(voterAddress))\n                throw new GovernanceException(\"Voter has already cast a vote on this proposal.\");\n\n            if (!_policies.All(p => p.ValidateVote(aggregate.Proposal, vote)))\n                throw new GovernanceException(\"One or more policies rejected the vote.\");\n\n            _lifecycleLock.EnterWriteLock();\n            try\n            {\n                aggregate.AddVote(vote);\n            }\n            finally\n            {\n                _lifecycleLock.ExitWriteLock();\n            }\n\n            _eventBus.Publish(new VoteCastEvent(vote));\n\n            return new VoteReceipt(vote, aggregate.Tally());\n        }\n        finally\n        {\n            _lifecycleLock.ExitUpgradeableReadLock();\n        }\n    }\n\n    public ProposalTally GetCurrentTally(Guid proposalId)\n    {\n        ThrowIfDisposed();\n\n        if (!_proposals.TryGetValue(proposalId, out var aggregate))\n            throw new ProposalNotFoundException(proposalId);\n\n        return aggregate.Tally();\n    }\n\n    public IEnumerable<Proposal> ListProposals(ProposalStatus? status = null)\n    {\n        ThrowIfDisposed();\n\n        return _proposals.Values\n                         .Select(a => a.Proposal)\n                         .Where(p => status is null || p.Status == status)\n                         .OrderByDescending(p => p.CreatedAt)\n                         .ToList(); // Materialize enumeration for thread-safety\n    }\n\n    #endregion\n\n    #region Event Handlers\n\n    private Task OnProposalCreatedAsync(ProposalCreatedEvent @event)\n    {\n        // Additional cross-cutting behavior could be executed here\n        // e.g., update search index, notify users, log analytics, etc.\n        return Task.CompletedTask;\n    }\n\n    private async Task OnProposalFinalizedAsync(ProposalFinalizedEvent @event)\n    {\n        // Dispatch post-finalization hooks in parallel\n        var tasks = _policies.Select(p => p.OnProposalFinalizedAsync(@event.Proposal, @event.Tally));\n        await Task.WhenAll(tasks).ConfigureAwait(false);\n    }\n\n    #endregion\n\n    #region Lifecycle\n\n    private async Task FinalizeAsync(ProposalAggregate aggregate, CancellationToken ct)\n    {\n        _lifecycleLock.EnterWriteLock();\n        try\n        {\n            if (aggregate.Proposal.Status is ProposalStatus.Finalized)\n                return; // Idempotent\n\n            var tally = aggregate.Tally();\n\n            var decision = _policies\n                .Select(p => p.EvaluateResult(aggregate.Proposal, tally))\n                .Aggregate(ProposalDecision.Undecided, CombineDecisions);\n\n            aggregate.Finalize(_clock.UtcNow, decision);\n\n            _eventBus.Publish(new ProposalFinalizedEvent(aggregate.Proposal, tally));\n        }\n        finally\n        {\n            _lifecycleLock.ExitWriteLock();\n        }\n\n        await Task.CompletedTask;\n    }\n\n    private static ProposalDecision CombineDecisions(ProposalDecision first, ProposalDecision second)\n    {\n        // If any policy rejects, the proposal is rejected.\n        if (first == ProposalDecision.Rejected || second == ProposalDecision.Rejected)\n            return ProposalDecision.Rejected;\n\n        // If any policy approves and none reject, approved.\n        if (first == ProposalDecision.Approved || second == ProposalDecision.Approved)\n            return ProposalDecision.Approved;\n\n        return ProposalDecision.Undecided;\n    }\n\n    #endregion\n\n    #region IDisposable\n\n    public void Dispose()\n    {\n        if (_disposed) return;\n\n        _lifecycleLock.Dispose();\n        _disposed = true;\n        GC.SuppressFinalize(this);\n    }\n\n    [MemberNotNull(nameof(_lifecycleLock))]\n    private void ThrowIfDisposed()\n    {\n        if (_disposed)\n            throw new ObjectDisposedException(nameof(GovernanceService));\n    }\n\n    #endregion\n}\n\n// ====================================================================================================================\n// Below are supporting types used by the GovernanceService. In a real-world project, each would live in its own file.\n// ====================================================================================================================\n\n#region Interfaces\n\n/// <summary>Public contract for interacting with on-chain governance.</summary>\npublic interface IGovernanceService\n{\n    Proposal CreateProposal(CreateProposalRequest request, CancellationToken ct = default);\n\n    VoteReceipt CastVote(Guid proposalId, VoteType voteType, string voterAddress, CancellationToken ct = default);\n\n    ProposalTally GetCurrentTally(Guid proposalId);\n\n    IEnumerable<Proposal> ListProposals(ProposalStatus? status = null);\n}\n\n/// <summary>\n///     Strategy interface for governance policy. Multiple policies can be evaluated sequentially.\n/// </summary>\npublic interface IGovernancePolicy\n{\n    bool ValidateProposal(Proposal proposal);\n\n    bool ValidateVote(Proposal proposal, Vote vote);\n\n    ProposalDecision EvaluateResult(Proposal proposal, ProposalTally tally);\n\n    Task OnProposalFinalizedAsync(Proposal proposal, ProposalTally tally);\n}\n\n#endregion\n\n#region Domain Models\n\npublic enum VoteType\n{\n    Abstain = 0,\n    Yes     = 1,\n    No      = 2\n}\n\npublic enum ProposalStatus\n{\n    Pending   = 0,\n    Finalized = 1\n}\n\npublic enum ProposalDecision\n{\n    Undecided = 0,\n    Approved  = 1,\n    Rejected  = 2\n}\n\npublic sealed record CreateProposalRequest(\n    string Title,\n    string Description,\n    DateTimeOffset VotingDeadline);\n\npublic sealed record Proposal(\n    Guid             Id,\n    string           Title,\n    string           Description,\n    DateTimeOffset   CreatedAt,\n    DateTimeOffset   VotingDeadline,\n    ProposalStatus   Status,\n    ProposalDecision Decision = ProposalDecision.Undecided,\n    DateTimeOffset?  FinalizedAt = null);\n\npublic sealed record Vote(\n    Guid           ProposalId,\n    string         VoterAddress,\n    VoteType       Type,\n    DateTimeOffset CastAt);\n\n/// <summary>A summary of vote counts for a proposal.</summary>\npublic sealed record ProposalTally(int YesCount, int NoCount, int AbstainCount)\n{\n    public int Total => YesCount + NoCount + AbstainCount;\n}\n\n/// <summary>\n///     Immutable receipt returned to the caller after their vote is committed.\n/// </summary>\npublic sealed record VoteReceipt(Vote Vote, ProposalTally CurrentTally);\n\n#endregion\n\n#region Aggregate Root\n\n/// <summary>\n///     Aggregate root encapsulating proposal state, votes, and invariants.\n///     Provides concurrent-safe access without explicit locks (controlled externally).\n/// </summary>\ninternal sealed class ProposalAggregate\n{\n    private readonly ConcurrentDictionary<string, Vote> _votes = new(StringComparer.Ordinal);\n\n    public ProposalAggregate(Proposal proposal) => Proposal = proposal;\n\n    public Proposal Proposal { get; private set; }\n\n    public bool HasVoted(string voterAddress) => _votes.ContainsKey(voterAddress);\n\n    public void AddVote(Vote vote)\n    {\n        if (!_votes.TryAdd(vote.VoterAddress, vote))\n            throw new GovernanceException(\"Duplicate vote detected.\");\n    }\n\n    public ProposalTally Tally()\n    {\n        var yes     = _votes.Values.Count(v => v.Type == VoteType.Yes);\n        var no      = _votes.Values.Count(v => v.Type == VoteType.No);\n        var abstain = _votes.Values.Count(v => v.Type == VoteType.Abstain);\n        return new ProposalTally(yes, no, abstain);\n    }\n\n    public void Finalize(DateTimeOffset finalizedAt, ProposalDecision decision)\n    {\n        Proposal = Proposal with\n        {\n            Status      = ProposalStatus.Finalized,\n            FinalizedAt = finalizedAt,\n            Decision    = decision\n        };\n    }\n}\n\n#endregion\n\n#region Policies\n\n/// <summary>\n///     Default simple-majority policy.\n///     Accepts proposal if YES > NO at the end of voting deadline.\n///     Requires a minimum turnout of 1 vote.\n/// </summary>\npublic sealed class SimpleMajorityPolicy : IGovernancePolicy\n{\n    public bool ValidateProposal(Proposal proposal)\n    {\n        if (proposal.VotingDeadline <= proposal.CreatedAt)\n            return false; // Deadline must be in the future\n\n        if (proposal.VotingDeadline - proposal.CreatedAt < TimeSpan.FromHours(1))\n            return false; // At least 1 hour voting window\n\n        return true;\n    }\n\n    public bool ValidateVote(Proposal proposal, Vote vote)\n    {\n        // Additional anti-sybil or stake-weight checks could be inserted here\n        return true;\n    }\n\n    public ProposalDecision EvaluateResult(Proposal proposal, ProposalTally tally)\n    {\n        if (tally.Total == 0)\n            return ProposalDecision.Rejected; // No participation \u2192 reject\n\n        return tally.YesCount > tally.NoCount\n            ? ProposalDecision.Approved\n            : ProposalDecision.Rejected;\n    }\n\n    public Task OnProposalFinalizedAsync(Proposal proposal, ProposalTally tally)\n    {\n        // Persistence or notifications can be handled here\n        return Task.CompletedTask;\n    }\n}\n\n#endregion\n\n#region Exceptions\n\npublic sealed class GovernanceException : Exception\n{\n    public GovernanceException(string message) : base(message) { }\n\n    public GovernanceException(string message, Exception inner) : base(message, inner) { }\n}\n\npublic sealed class ProposalNotFoundException : GovernanceException\n{\n    public ProposalNotFoundException(Guid proposalId)\n        : base($\"Proposal '{proposalId}' was not found.\") { }\n}\n\n#endregion\n```\n",

ct).ConfigureAwait(false);\n            return (T)payload;\n        }\n\n        public async Task<object> ReceiveAsync(Type type, int bytes, CancellationToken ct = default)\n        {\n            var buffer = _bufferPool.Rent(bytes);\n            try\n            {\n                await FillBufferAsync(buffer, bytes, ct).ConfigureAwait(false);\n                return _bufferPool.Rent(sizeof(int));\n            try\n            {\n                await FillBufferAsync(lenBytes, sizeof(int), ct).ConfigureAwait(false);\n                var headerLen = headerLen, ct).ConfigureAwait(false);\n                    return JsonSerializer.Deserialize<MessageHeader>(headerBuffer.AsSpan(0, headerLen), _jsonOpts)!;\n                }\n                finally\n                {\n                    _bufferPool.Return(headerBuffer);\n                }\n            }\n            finally\n            {\n                _bufferPool.Return(lenBytes);\n            }\n        }\n\n        private async Task FillBufferAsync(byte[] buffer, int count, CancellationToken ct)\n        {\n            var offset = 0;\n            while (offset < count)\n            {\n                var read = await _stream.ReadAsync(buffer.AsMemory(offset, count - offset), ct).ConfigureAwait(false);\n                if (read == 0) throw new IOException(\"Remote closed connection.\");\n                offset += read;\n            }\n        }\n\n        #endregion\n\n        public PeerInfo ToPeerInfo() => new(NodeId, RemoteEndPoint);\n\n        public void It is the single source of truth for the\n//  current epoch, slot, validator set, and vote receipts, enabling other\n//  modules (staking, governance, API gateway) to interrogate consensus state\n//  without directly coupling to the engine implementation.\n// -----------------------------------------------------------------------------\n\nusing System;\nusing System.Collections.Concurrent;\nusing System.Collections.Generic;\nusing System.Diagnostics.CodeAnalysis;\nusing System.Linq;\nusing System.Threading;\nusing System.Threading.Tasks;\nusing Microsoft.Extensions.Logging;\nusing UtilityChain.Common.Guards;\nusing UtilityChain.Common.Time;\nusing UtilityChain.Messaging;\nusing UtilityChain.Persistence;\n\nnamespace UtilityChain.Consensus;\n\n/// <summary>\n/// Represents the authoritative, thread-safe context object that maintains\n/// the volatile consensus state for the running node.  This includes\n/// coordination of epochs/slots, vote receipts, validator liveness tracking,\n/// and delegated execution of the underlying consensus algorithm.\n/// </summary>\npublic sealed class    finally\n        {\n            _stateLock.ExitReadLock();\n        }\n\n        var slotStart   = _clock.UtcNow;\n        var slotEnd     = slotStart.Add(snapshot.SlotDuration);\n\n        _logger.LogDebug(\"Executing slot {Slot} of epoch {Epoch}.\", snapshot.SlotIndex, snapshot.Epoch);\n\n        // Strategy pattern: delegate to the configured consensus engine\n        var result = BlockProposedEvent(proposal.Block));\n                break;\n\n            case SlotResult.Empty:\n                _logger.LogTrace(\"Slot {Slot} completed with no block proposal.\", snapshot.SlotIndex);\n                break;\n        }\n\n        // Rotate to next slot\n        _stateLock.EnterWriteLock();\n        try\n        {\n            var nextSlot = (snapshot.SlotIndex                Epoch       = epoch,\n                SlotStarted = slotStart\n            };\n        }\n        finally\n        {\n            _stateLock.ExitWriteLock();\n        }\n\n        var
